< review>
Nothing easy about managing any business through these crazy, uncertain times. I personally am grateful to have a place like Peltzer Winery and the Pumpkin Patch who are doing an amazing job navigating through the craziness so we have something to look forward to. During the week when it's less busy I like to go and relax with a glass of wine (that Meritage is sooooo good). I also think it's super cool that they've spent the time to spread all the seating areas out and coordinate activities on the farm that support social distancing. Some people struggle with the mask requirement and I imagine it's difficult to make us all happy and comfortable but all in all, I think the Peltzer family and team are doing an amazing job. Grateful for y'all!!!!< /review>

< Review>
Surprisingly affordable because you can have an entree with several sides below $10. This place seems to be a late arrival in the Hawaiian BBQ craze of yesteryear, but to be fair, it doesn't come off as trying to sell you Hawaiian dishes as a novelty. Try the dishes because they are visually enticing, affordably priced, and refreshingly different at least as far as the food offerings on this strip by the subway is concerned.<//Review>

Okay... I'm having a bit of a hard time trying to figure out how to explain  how I feel about this place. I've been to two of these locations. The first one was how I expected it to be. Not great,  but also not completely terrible.  I went to this location, after I got done eating ( I despise wasting food) I knew I was never going to come back to any of these places  on my own merits. I ordered a chicken cutlet. Its such a simple thing.  I don't know what on earth happened but it tasted and felt like they forgot about it in the fryer but still decided to serve it to me anyway. This combined with a pile of overcooked, mushy rice, and a laughably tiny glob of macaroni salad, for the price I paid for it, was almost insulting.  I spent the whole meal just washing it down with my beverage.  At least the woman at the counter was nice? She did her job well. That should be acknowledged. I was not displeased with the service. Just the food they served.   I hope they adopt some better quality control in the future because that was a real shame.<//text>

< Text>
My daughter and I worked with Cheryl of Tehama to have her wedding there in April 2021. We met with Cheryl and found her to be very professional.we consulted vendors who loved working with Cheryl and confirmed she was very qualified to handle our wedding. We were very excited after meeting her and she answered our questions and again we felt very comfortable with her.

We asked her if she was committed to doing our wedding in April and she said she would be retiring in about a year but promised us she would be there in April to coordinate the wedding.

She sent us a deposit form and we sent the check. Tehama, with out letting us know, terminated Cheryl and then cashed our deposit check. They did not let us know that Cheryl would not be doing our wedding, or tell us who her replacement would be. They failed to disclose this information and deposited our check anyways.  After a few weeks of no response from Cheryl or Tehama, we contacted the Food and Beverage manager who said Cheryl was no longer there and new nothing about our wedding. We contacted vendors who said they were very concerned about Cheryl being gone and that we should be concerned.

We lost confidence and asked for our deposit back.

Tom the general manager and I discussed the matter and my daughter and I had discussed the refund..

Tom came back and agreed the termination had happened during our making the deposit but has defused to return the whole deposit. The way Tehama has handled this has devastated our daughter and we both feel that Tehama did not properly disclose to us Cheryl would not be there and cashed our deposit anyways.

They misrepresented who we would have at Tehama and want to keep the deposit. We will update this if Tehama properly refunds the deposit to my daughter. If they don‚Äôt you should not trust them with your very special event.<//Text>

<Text>I am a Monterey wedding planner and I absolutely love working with Tehama and weddings here are nothing short of perfection.
I have planned several weddings at Tehama and always really enjoyed working with all their incredible staff but also everyone that works in banquets is kind, friendly, and so wonderful at what they do.
The property itself is beautiful, from the minute you enter and see their beautiful courtyard with the gardens and fountains its just breathtaking.
The ceremony deck offers unencumbered views of the ocean and Monterey Bay, while the golf course is nestled in the golden hills of Carmel Valley.
Their food is also really top notch. Often beautiful venues fall flat when it comes to the food but not Tehama. They really deliver a stellar experience all around. I highly recommend them if you are looking for the perfect venue for your wedding.</Text></record></dataset><record>

< review>
We love coming here! They definitely have the best poke in the area and it's a plus that the staff is overly friendly. Their ingredients and fish are always super fresh and vibrant, which I can't say for a lot of the other poke shops close by...probably since they have less orders their food sits around longer.

Another thing we love about this spot is that they do collaborations bowls with popular chefs from other famous restaurants around LA so the menu is always changing! I personally usually get the fish bowls and they're always spot on but if I'm feeling I want to go more healthy I go with the Plant-Based bowls which have more veggies and are lighter on the ole gut.<//review>

< Review>
This store is the absolute best!if you have a chance, look at the attached pictures. Words do not begin to describe how large a selection of rums, whiskey, scotch, cognac, brandy, gin, etc. This store is slightly smaller than their main store off of El cajon boulevard.

If you are looking for something Specific to either enjoy, or as a gift, kegel bottle is definitely a place worth visiting. Regardless of the type of alcoholic beverage you are looking for, they will have that selection.  The prices they charge for their selection are completely reasonable, too. They do have some drinks that they will have on sale. On the hole, everything in there is completely reasonable in price with a selection that isn't matched anywhere else in the San Diego area!</Review>

<Pics>None< /Pics><Review>This store is selling sakes that are "EXPIRED and HAVE GONE BAD".  Please don't go into this store unless you want to walk out with bottles of expired alcohol.  I purchased three bottles of sparkling sake on 12/21/2012 from there and found out later that they were produced in 2009 and should be consumed within 120 days.  Plus, the sakes were not being stored properly.  They were just sitting on the self at room temperature when clearly on the bottle's label, "Keep Refrigerated"  No wonder not only there's no bubble when opened plus the taste was awful.  I even asked the owner about the expiration date because I saw a set of date (21.9.24) on the cap.  The owner assured that the sakes are fine and even if that's the expiration date, it should be either year of 2021/2024 so they are all good.  Later I googled and found out that the number 21 is era in Japan which corresponds to year of 2009 in Western era. < review>
Had high hopes for one of the only 5-star repair shops. Went in for a screen & camera swap for my iPhone X on 1/25, paid $140 for the screen, but turned out to be a mediocre LCD display instead of the OLED panel it should have been. Thought it was a mistake, but it turns out an OLED panel is an extra $40 charge.

Waited a week for them to order it and was willing to pay the extra fee. Eventually went to the shop and had it swapped out, but in the process they damaged one of the sensors on the front of the phone, so now Face ID doesn't work. They said they'd do some research to find what's wrong, and if needed, I'd drop my phone off for a few days to have their micro-solder tech fix it, while I use a loaner phone provided by them. They were going to call me in a few days to schedule this.

I initially went to the shop on January 25th. It is now March 5th, and I still haven't received a call asking me to come in so my phone can be repaired. Have been texting and calling them all throughout, with repeated promises that they'd get back to me soon. Texted the owner again this Monday and was told he'd contact me "in the next day or two". It's been three days and I'm not very hopeful. At this point, I'm not sure I'd trust leaving my phone with them, because I'm not sure when I'd get it back.

I understand the owner has been having some difficulties outside of work that make him unavailable, and I sympathize with that. However, there's been hardly any communication, and after weeks, my phone's Face ID still doesn't work thanks to whatever happened during the repair. At least they didn't charge me the extra fee for the OLED...

PS. At least post accurate hours! Stopped by at about 4pm a couple weeks ago, on a weekday, and the place was closed? Okay.<//review>
